Can the customer see my trackers?

=

No, the customer cannot see your trackers! =F0=9F=94=92

Your referral tracker is= completely private because:

  1. LocalStorage is private= - All data is stored in YOUR browser only, on YOUR device
  2. No backend/database - There's no server storing or sharing data
  3. Client-side only - Everything stays on your computer/phone
  4. Not visible to visitors= - When someone visits your site, they see the same educational co= ntent and referral buttons, but they cannot see:
    • Your referral list
    • Your progress bar
    • Your milestone achievements
    • Any names or contact info you'v= e entered

What customers DO see:

  • Home page with your intro
  • Educational Medicare content
  • "Connect with EOS" buttons
  • Disclaimer

What ONLY YOU see (when = you access the Tracker section):

  • All your referral entries
  • Progress tracking
  • Export/Import functions
  • Milestone achievements

Think of it like a journal that = only appears when YOU open it. Each visitor has their own separate browser = storage, so your data never mixes with theirs.

If you want to access your track= er from multiple devices (phone, tablet, computer), just use the Ex= port button to download your data, then Import it= on your other device! =F0=9F=93=B1=F0=9F=92=BB

How do I share the App?

Great question! Here are several ways to share your Medicare Refer= ral Hub app:

=F0=9F=8C=90 Best Options for Sharing:

Option 1= : Host it as a Website (Recommended)

You'll need to save the code as = an HTML file and host it online:

Free Hosting Services:

  • GitHub Pages (= free, easy) - github.com
  • Netlify (free,= drag & drop) - netlify.com
  • Vercel (free) = - vercel.com
  • Google Sites o= r Wix (free tiers available)

Steps:

  1. Copy all the code from the arti= fact
  2. Save it as index.html on your = computer
  3. Upload to one of the free hosti= ng services above
  4. You'll get a URL like: yourname.githu= b.io or yoursite.netlify.app
  5. Share that link via text, email= , social media, QR code, etc.

Option 2= : Send the File Directly

  • Save the code as index.html
  • Email it as an attachment
  • Recipients can open it in their= browser (Chrome, Safari, Firefox, etc.)
  • Note: They'll = each have their own blank app; they won't see your tracker data

Option 3= : Create a QR Code

Once you have a hosted URL:

  • Use a free QR code generator (q= r-code-generator.com)
  • Print it on business cards, fly= ers, or display on your phone
  • People scan and go directly to = your app

Option 4= : Social Media Sharing

Post the link on:

  • Facebook
  • Instagram bio
  • LinkedIn profile
  • WhatsApp status
  • Email signature
